The primary stack protection implementations are:\\n\\n### 1. StackProtector Pass (llvm/lib/CodeGen/StackProtector.cpp)\\nThe main LLVM pass that inserts stack protector checks into functions. This file contains:\\n- **StackProtectorPass**: The new PassInfoMixin-based pass class for use with the new PassManager\\n- **StackProtector**: The legacy FunctionPass class for backward compatibility\\n- **InsertStackProtectors()**: Core static function that performs the actual insertion of prologue code (which stores a random canary to the stack) and epilogue code (which checks if the canary has been modified and calls __stack_chk_fail if it has). SafeStack Pass (llvm/lib/CodeGen/SafeStack.cpp)\\nImplements the SafeStack pass that separates stack allocations into safe and unsafe stacks to prevent certain classes of buffer overflow attacks. This file contains:\\n- **SafeStackPass**: The new pass infrastructure class\\n- **SafeStack**: The main implementation class that performs the actual stack separation work\\n- **SafeStackLegacyPass**: The legacy FunctionPass wrapper\\n\\nKey methods in SafeStack class:\\n- `SafeStack::run()`: Main entry point that orchestrates the safe/unsafe stack separation\\n- `SafeStack::findInsts()`: Locates all static allocas, dynamic allocas, return instructions, and stack restore points\\n- `SafeStack::moveStaticAllocasToUnsafeStack()`: Allocates space for unsafe static allocas on the unsafe stack\\n- `SafeStack::moveDynamicAllocasToUnsafeStack()`: Replaces dynamic allocas with runtime allocation on the unsafe stack\\n- `SafeStack::checkStackGuard()`: Validates stack guard consistency and calls __stack_chk_fail if compromised\\n- `SafeStack::getStackGuard()`: Retrieves the current stack canary value\\n- `SafeStack::IsSafeStackAlloca()`: Determines whether an allocation is safe or requires unsafe stack separation\\n\\nThe SafeStack implementation splits the stack into two regions:\\n- **Safe Stack**: Regular stack for memory-safe accesses\\n- **Unsafe Stack**: Explicitly allocated and managed stack for unsafe access patterns\\n\\n### 3. if modified, creates a call to __stack_chk_fail\\n3. **Safe Stack Separation** (SafeStack): Identifies unsafe memory access patterns and moves those allocations to a separately managed unsafe stack\\n4. **Layout** (SafeStackLayout): Manages efficient placement of stack objects with proper alignment\\n5. **Runtime** (__stack_chk_fail): Handles detection and reports stack smashing attacks\\n\\nThese mechanisms combine to provide defense-in-depth against stack buffer overflow attacks in compiled code.\"\n}\n"},"caller":{"type":"direct"}}],"stop_reason":null,"stop_sequence":null,"usage":{"input_tokens":9,"cache_creation_input_tokens":3382,"cache_read_input_tokens":84985,"cache_creation":{"ephemeral_5m_input_tokens":0,"ephemeral_1h_input_tokens":3382},"output_tokens":1,"service_tier":"standard","inference_geo":"not_available"},"context_management":null},"parent_tool_use_id":null,"session_id":"d001f217-35a0-4499-b57f-9f4dd7f89a3e","uuid":"3f4ab89e-128c-47b1-ab99-e1340433993c"}

The function generates code that stores a random value onto the stack before local variables are allocated and checks this value upon exiting, calling __stack_chk_fail if it has changed.\\n- **CreateFailBB()**: Creates a basic block for failure handling that invokes __stack_chk_fail\\n- **SSPLayoutAnalysis** and **SSPLayoutInfo**: Analysis pass and info class that determine which functions require stack protection based on buffer sizes, variable types, and function attributes\\n\\nKey methods:\\n- `PreservedAnalyses StackProtectorPass::run(Function &F, FunctionAnalysisManager &FAM)`: New-style pass entry point\\n- `bool StackProtector::runOnFunction(Function &Fn)`: Legacy pass entry point\\n- The pass requires the LibcallLoweringInfo analysis to determine the appropriate runtime library calls to use\\n\\n### 2. SafeStack Pass (llvm/lib/CodeGen/SafeStack.cpp)\\nImplements the SafeStack pass that separates stack allocations into safe and unsafe stacks to prevent certain classes of buffer overflow attacks. This file contains:\\n- **SafeStackPass**: The new pass infrastructure class\\n- **SafeStack**: The main implementation class that performs the actual stack separation work\\n- **SafeStackLegacyPass**: The legacy FunctionPass wrapper\\n\\nKey methods in SafeStack class:\\n- `SafeStack::run()`: Main entry point that orchestrates the safe/unsafe stack separation\\n- `SafeStack::findInsts()`: Locates all static allocas, dynamic allocas, return instructions, and stack restore points\\n- `SafeStack::moveStaticAllocasToUnsafeStack()`: Allocates space for unsafe static allocas on the unsafe stack\\n- `SafeStack::moveDynamicAllocasToUnsafeStack()`: Replaces dynamic allocas with runtime allocation on the unsafe stack\\n- `SafeStack::checkStackGuard()`: Validates stack guard consistency and calls __stack_chk_fail if compromised\\n- `SafeStack::getStackGuard()`: Retrieves the current stack canary value\\n- `SafeStack::IsSafeStackAlloca()`: Determines whether an allocation is safe or requires unsafe stack separation\\n\\nThe SafeStack implementation splits the stack into two regions:\\n- **Safe Stack**: Regular stack for memory-safe accesses\\n- **Unsafe Stack**: Explicitly allocated and managed stack for unsafe access patterns\\n\\n### 3. Header Files\\n**llvm/include/llvm/CodeGen/StackProtector.h** declares:\\n- `class SSPLayoutInfo`: Information about required stack protection layout for a function\\n- `class SSPLayoutAnalysis`: Analysis pass that determines stack protection requirements\\n- `class StackProtectorPass`: The new-style pass interface\\n\\n**llvm/include/llvm/CodeGen/SafeStack.h** declares:\\n- `class SafeStackPass`: New pass infrastructure interface with `run(Function &F, FunctionAnalysisManager &FAM)` method\\n\\n### 4. SafeStack Layout Classes\\n**llvm/lib/CodeGen/SafeStackLayout.h** declares:\\n- `class StackLayout`: Computes the layout of unsafe stack frames, managing stack regions and object placement\\n\\n**llvm/lib/CodeGen/SafeStackLayout.cpp** implements:\\n- `StackLayout::addObject()`: Adds objects to the stack layout\\n- `StackLayout::layoutObject()`: Places objects in stack regions with proper alignment\\n- Stack region management for coloring and efficient space usage\\n\\n### 5. __stack_chk_fail Runtime Implementation\\n**libc/src/compiler/generic/__stack_chk_fail.cpp** provides:\\n- `void __stack_chk_fail(void)`: The runtime function called when a stack protector check fails. This is a [[noreturn]] function that:\\n  1. Writes \\\"stack smashing detected\\\\n\\\" to stderr via `LIBC_NAMESPACE::write_to_stderr()`\\n  2. Calls `LIBC_NAMESPACE::abort()` to terminate the program\\n  3. Defines `__stack_chk_guard`: The global canary value used for stack protector checks (initialized to 0xa9fff01234)\\n\\n**libc/src/compiler/__stack_chk_fail.h** declares:\\n- The `extern \\\"C\\\"` declaration of the `__stack_chk_fail()` function\\n\\n### Instrumentation Integration\\nWhile there is no dedicated stack frame protection instrumentation pass in `llvm/lib/Transforms/Instrumentation/`, the stack protection is integrated through:\\n- **StackProtector** pass running in the code generation pipeline (CodeGen phase)\\n- **SafeStack** pass running as a CodeGen pass\\n- **AddressSanitizer.cpp** and **HWAddressSanitizer.cpp** in the Instrumentation directory include stack safety analysis integration (ClUseStackSafety flag) that leverages stack safety information to avoid redundant instrumentation\\n\\n### Architecture Summary\\nThe stack protection mechanism works as follows:\\n1. **Analysis Phase**: SSPLayoutAnalysis determines which functions require protection based on function attributes and local variable types\\n2. **Insertion Phase** (StackProtector): \\n   - Prologue: Loads a random canary from the stack guard global and stores it onto the function's stack\\n   - Epilogue: Reloads and compares the stored canary; if modified, creates a call to __stack_chk_fail\\n3. **Safe Stack Separation** (SafeStack): Identifies unsafe memory access patterns and moves those allocations to a separately managed unsafe stack\\n4. **Layout** (SafeStackLayout): Manages efficient placement of stack objects with proper alignment\\n5. **Runtime** (__stack_chk_fail): Handles detection and reports stack smashing attacks\\n\\nThese mechanisms combine to provide defense-in-depth against stack buffer overflow attacks in compiled code.\"\n}\n","structuredPatch":[],"originalFile":null}}
